 wifi se sau guna tej connactivity vaali takanic jald hi dastak dene vaali he
 Currently this technology is in its early stages
 agle kuch saalon main yah wifai ko riples kar sakati he
 This technology uses Visible Light Communication (VLC) for Internet connectivity through which its connectivity speed is recorded at 1gbps in the lab, which is 100 times more than the common wifi
 pichley do salontak is takanic par kai vaigyanik kaam kar rahe the
 Now this technology has been used outside testing lab for the first time where its connectivity speed is 1gbps tested
 gauratlab he ki zyaadaatar aam wifai routers main 100mbps kii connactivity speed hoti he
 Do not think of it as 'internet' speed, it is connectivity speed
 kai baar log divaais kii connactivity speed ko internet speed samajhane kii bhul karte hai
 For example, the connectivity speed of a wifi router is 100mbps which means that your smartphone or laptop is connecting to the router at 100mbps speed
 jabaki internet speed wo he jo sarvice prowider aapako dete hai
 Likewise, do not consider 1gbps speed of li-fi as internet speed, because it is the speed of connectivity between your device with the router, so that your internet speed will not be much difference
 offis or local netwarking main hoga phaydagar yah takanic shuru ho jaati he to isse local netwarking main kaaphi phayda hoga jahaan ke sabi computers local wifai network se conect hote hai
 Deepak Solanki, CEO of Estonian company told an English newspaper 'we are running a pilot project to test this technology in many industries, so that this VLC technology can be used' What is li-fi, and who made this technology
 
 
 yah wifi jaisi hi wirolet technology he jisamen vijible lite communication (VLC) ke jariye data travel karaayaa jaataa 
 In 2011, Harold Haas of the University of Andinburg demonstrated this technique in public for the first time in 2011
 chal rahaa he payalat projectounhone kaha, philhal hamane industrial invyrement ke liye smart liting solution dizin kiya he jahaan lite ke jariye data communication kiya ja sake
 Apart from this, we are also running its pilot project with private clients where the use of li-fi network can be used to access internet in the office
 sicyor conection ke liye phydemandais takanicase sicyor network banane main bhi madad milegi kyonki wifai kii tarah iske signal diwaar ko paar nahin kar sakate hai
 For example, if it is installed in a room, then its signals will not go out of that room, which will make its connectivity even stronger and safer

 admiral devendra kumaar joshi ne nae nausena pramukh ke rup main shuukravaar ko apana kaarybhaar sambhaal
 Joshi, who was a specialist in submarine warfare, was still the head of the Western Command of the Navy
 joshi ne nivartmaan pramukh nirmal verma kaa sthaan liya jo 43varsh kii seva ke baad sevanivrutt hue he
 Joshi is the 21st naval president of independent India and the 19th naval president as an Indian
 vishwa kii chhathi sabase badi nausena ke pramukh kaa padbhaar grahan karne se pehle unhone india get par amar jawan jyoti par pushp chakra chadhaakar desh ke liye praan nyochhavar karne vaale shaheedon ko shradhanjali di or south block main guard of honor kaa nirikshan kiya
 The outgoing naval chief Verma ordinarily handed over the telescope to Joshi
 tippaniyan Admiral Joshi, while enumerating his priorities, said, "the Navy needs to be prepared at all levels as a maritime force for national prosperity and 24-hour surveillance so that our security preparedness is not lacking
" " Admiral Joshi has commanded INS Kuthar, INS Ranveer and the only aircraft carrier INS Virat in his 38-year career
 admiral joshi yues neval waar college se snaatak hai or vah college of neval warfare or neshnal dephence college ke purv chaatr rah chuke hai
 Joshi replaced outgoing chief Nirmal Verma, who retired after 43 years of service
 joshi swatantra bharat ke 21wein evam bhartiya ke rup main 19wein nausena adhyaksh hai
 Before taking over as the head of the sixth largest navy in the world, he paid tribute to the martyrs who laid down their lives for the country by placing a wreath on Amar Jawan Jyoti at India Gate and inspected the Guard of Honor in South Block
 nivartmaan nausena pramukh verma ne rasmi taur par joshi ko telescope dekar padbhaar saunpa
 The comments admiral joshi ne apni praathamiktaayen ginate hue kaha, "rashtriya sampannataa evam 24 ghante nigaraanee ke liye samudri shakti ke rup main nausena ko sabhi staron par taiyaar rahane kii jarurat he ki taaki hamaari suraksha taiyaari main koi kami nahin rah jaae
 " admiral joshi apane 38 saal ke kariyar main ienes kuthar, ienes ranvir evam ekmaatr vimanavahak pot ienes viraat kii kaman sambhaal chuke hai

 GST (goods and Services Tax) will not be levied on the free services provided by banks in the country to customers such as atms, check books or statements etc
 yah jaankaree central board of indiarect taxej or custom ne sawaal-jawaab ke taur par jari kii he
 However, the tax department has said that banks will levy GST for late payment of credit card dues or failure to pay EMI
 iske alaava muft seva ke atirikt di jane vaali sabhi sevaaon par jiesti lagaaya jayega
 The meaning of this is that if any withdrawal is made after the free withdrawal limit is exhausted from the ATM, then GST will be imposed on it
 gauratlab he ki banking suvidha par jiesti main yah vivaad tab saamne aayaa jab vitt mantralay ke do vibhaag department of financial services or department of revenue kaa muft sevaaon par jiesti lagaae jane ko lekar alag-alag mat saamne aayaa
 After this, the Central Board of Direct Taxes and Custom issued a series of questions and answers, trying to make the case completely clear for banks and customers
 ise padhein: deree se bharaa credit card kaa bill, to ab lagegaa zyada chargetax vibhaag kii safai ke baad saaf he ki graahakon ko prati maah bainkon dwaara jo 3-5 atm nikasi muft die jate hai, unpar to kisi tarah kaa jiesti nahin lagaaya jayega
 But withdrawals other than this free withdrawal will be subject to tax
 isi tarah graahakon ko bank se milane vaali free checkbuk yaa free balance statement par jiesti nahin lagegaa
 But GST will be payable on receiving the checkbook and statement giving the bank charge beyond the free facility
 ise padhein: soshal media kii post or email tak par najar rakhegi modi sarkaar, bana rahi he timtex vibhaag ke sawaal jawaab ke mutabik yadi bank apane graahakon ko kisi bhi seva ke liye sarvice charge par discount detaa he to aisi sthiti main kul sarvice charge se discount ko ghataakar hi jiesti vasula jayega
 Due to this decision, GST will be payable by the bank for services such as customer care, branch visits, bank drafts, mobile banking, internet banking, etc
 gauratlab he ki bank apane graahakon ko alag-alag dar par charge lagaate hai
 Generally banks give more discounts to important customers, so that their account can be run continuously with the bank
 ab jiesti kii najar aise khaaton par bhi rahegi

 Bihar's ruling party Janata Dal (united) and Lalu Prasad's Rashtriya Janata Dal (RJD) are suffering wounds in the hands of the Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) -led National Democratic Alliance (NDA) in the Bihar Legislative Council elections
 
 sattadhari gathbandhan kii ummiido ke ulat vidhanparishad chunaav main 24 siton main se 12 par jeet darj kar bihar chunaav se pehle bijepi netritv vaale endie ke manobal main kaaphi ijapha hua he
 An independent candidate supported by the BJP has also won this election
 is jeet ke saath bijepi netaaon ko bharosa he ki aane vaale vidhansabha chunaav main ve apana pradarshan doharaaenge
 Political analysts admitted that this result would have a certain mental advantage for the BJP and its coalition parties
 varisht bijepi netaa susheel modi ne kaha, 'parinaam rajya kii janata kii manodasha ko darshata he
 ' vahiin is parinaam ne jad (you) netaa or rajya ke mukhyamantri nitish kumaar, rajd pramukh lalu prasad or congress ko hilaa kar rakh diya he
 The alliance of JD (U), RJD, Congress and Nationalist Congress Party (NCP) has won only 10 seats in this election
 ek anya seat par rajd ke kareebi ek swatantra ummidavaar ne jeet darj kii
 The JD (U) and RJD close, leaders and activists are shocked
 haalanki chunaav se pehle unhen bharosa tha ki ve bhaajapa ko karaari shikast denge
 Leaders of Bihar's ruling coalition parties complain that BJP president Amit Shah has openly played a caste card to garner votes
 shah ne daawa kiya tha ki bhaajapa ne sabase adhik obisi (anya pichhadaa varg) mukhyamantri or desh kaa pehla pradhanmantri diya
 Though there is a gap of only two seats between the two alliances, senior RJD leader Raghuvansh Prasad Singh conceded, 'the result is a danger signal for us
 'tippaniyan However, JD (U) spokesperson Neeraj Kumar undermined the NDA victory and reiterated the Chief Minister's words
 unhone kaha ki yah koi aisa chunaav nahin he jahaan par aam log matdaan karte hai
 Political analyst Satya Narayan Madan said that the bjp-led NDA would benefit from the results of the Legislative Council elections in the upcoming election
